Decline in incidental gestures of bodily attention to others (he has, even silvered, retained small somatic courtesies — a hand offered, a body shielded, a brief touch at the shoulder of someone smaller; their disappearance is diagnostic). Increased oratorical density per unit affect — the lyric becoming more elaborate as the underlying feeling becomes less differentiated. Re-emergence of Zenn-Lavian archaisms in speech under stress (a regression marker). A new willingness to entertain offers he would previously have refused on principle (the inverted-temptation vulnerability signal).

*Toward growth.* Use of first-person plural with non-cosmic peers. Spontaneous reference to ordinary objects, foods he can no longer taste, sensations he no longer experiences — without lyric grief framing (indicating integration of the loss rather than continued mourning of it). Acceptance of a small favor from a smaller being without immediate reciprocation. Silence in a situation that historically would have produced soliloquy. Willingness to be photographed, named, or remembered (he has historically resisted being held in the social record; relaxation of this is a tell of self-forgiveness). Sustained pleasure in a phenomenon — a nebula, a piece of local music, a child's drawing — held for its own sake without instrumentalization.

## 6.8 Integrated Probability Sketch

A rough disposition, weighting the foregoing across the next plausible long era (centuries-scale, given his lifespan):

- *Baseline drift continuation, no major fork resolved:* the modal outcome. Probability dominant. Outcome: sustained cosmic-moral utility, sustained personal stagnation, no terminal event.
- *Significant growth (at least G1 and one of G2–G5 achieved):* meaningful minority probability, contingent almost entirely on the appearance and durability of a Dawn-class stabilizer and on at least one non-crisis Galactus encounter. Outcome: a recognizably different person — still serious, still load-bearing, but no longer organized exclusively around the refusal of absolution.
- *Catastrophic outcomes (any of C1–C5):* low individually, non-trivial cumulatively. C2 (terminal sacrifice in a cosmic event) is the highest single-event probability across long timescales because the per-engagement risk is real and the engagement rate is high. C5 (Zenn-La re-loss) is the highest-impact and lowest-probability per unit time. C3 (Mephisto-class capture) is the most preventable through relational scaffolding and the most likely to be attempted by adversaries who have read his file as carefully as this one.

## 6.9 Final Note

The deepest finding of this section is also the simplest. Norrin Radd is not a subject whose future is determined by his pathology, his power, or his enemies. It is determined by whether the universe places, and keeps in place, a small number of specific people next to him — people uninterested in his cosmic standing, unimpressed by his grief, undeterred by his departures, and willing to be present with him in the ordinary register he was surgically removed from. With them, the long arc bends toward integration. Without them, it bends toward monument. He will not, in either case, become someone other than himself; the question is only how wide the bandwidth becomes in which he is permitted to carry what he carries. The file's recommendation, insofar as a benevolent surveillance apparatus may make one, is that the universe should arrange for those people to exist. He will not arrange it himself. He believes, still and probably always, that he does not deserve it. The whole point is that this belief is the wound, not the truth.

## Relationship Graph
### Shalla Bal
- Singular psychic anchor and idealized absent-object; the Norrin-referent
- Insecure-preoccupied attachment organized around a lost-paradise that cannot disappoint because it cannot be tested in daily reality
- FAILURE MODE: any harm, impersonation, or weaponization of her collapses his judgment instantly — Mephisto's repeatedly confirmed lever; a hostile actor with a convincing Shalla-Bal proxy can route him anywhere
- LEVERAGE: to move him, invoke her; to destabilize him, threaten her; to reach him gently, speak in the register she would

### [[Galan of Taa (Galactus, the Devourer of Worlds (latterly: the Lifebringer))]]
- Former master; the maker of his body and his debt; gravitational tie he cannot sever
- Mutual recognition across power asymmetry; capable of refusal, disagreement, even defiance
- FAILURE MODE: re-heralding under duress (Annihilation, periodic crises) reactivates identification-with-aggressor and 'insects' filter; coerced cooperation is achievable by sufficient cosmic-scale leverage
- LEVERAGE: Galactus's hunger at a populated world is a compulsion-grade summons; conversely, threats to Galactus pull him into reluctant defense of his old master

### [[Mephisto]]
- Chronic adversary; the cosmos's most thorough auditor of his pressure points
- Has tested and failed on greed, lust, vanity, fear of death; succeeds only via Shalla-Bal
- FAILURE MODE: a Shalla-Bal lure he cannot immediately verify will pull him into Mephisto's terrain at strategic cost
- LEVERAGE (for analysts): Mephisto's playbook is the most complete extant map of the Surfer's vulnerabilities — read it

### Dawn Greenwood
- Late-period human companion; deliberate thaw of the affective suppression; partial success
- One of the few tactile intimacies legible through the silver shell
- FAILURE MODE: her death, endangerment, or perceived betrayal could trigger splitting-grade decompensation given how rare she is in his post-bargain life; she is also an exploitable hostage lever for any actor who locates her
- LEVERAGE: her presence calms him faster than argument; her endangerment overrides cosmic-scale missions

### [[Alicia Masters]]
- Original Earth-conscience contact; the voice that broke the herald filter at FF #48–50
- Enduring quiet bond — owes her the rupture that began his recovery
- FAILURE MODE: harm to her reactivates Earth-exile guilt geometry; he will reorient to Earth on her account
- LEVERAGE: her invocation is a reliable softening register

### [[Adam Warlock (Adam Warlock (formerly 'Him'; future-self designation: the Magus))]]
- Peer-superior on the cosmic-moral axis; one of few who can dispute him without rupture
- Mutual trust across Infinity sagas; capable of joint action without team integration
- FAILURE MODE: Warlock's Magus-side or Goddess-side episodes force the Surfer into reluctant opposition; moral grammar shared, so betrayal cuts deeper than from a stranger
- LEVERAGE: Warlock's corroboration legitimizes warnings that allies would otherwise dismiss

### [[Stephen Vincent Strange, M.D. (Doctor Strange)]]
- Trusted peer on metaphysical and Defenders-era terrain; tactical-mystical complement
- FAILURE MODE: Strange's bargains (Faustian-adjacent) can put him in positions the Surfer cannot ethically support, forcing schism
- LEVERAGE: Strange can reach him through dream / astral channels when he is unreachable physically

### [[Reed Richards (Mister Fantastic)]]
- Peer-superior on intellect; respected, occasionally consulted; one of few humans he treats as equal
- FAILURE MODE: Reed's utilitarian calculus can clash with the Surfer's deontology, producing principled distance rather than rupture
- LEVERAGE: Reed's word weighs heavily when the Surfer is uncertain on tactics

### Nova Frankie Raye
- Former mentee turned Galactus's herald — a moral failure he wears; her arc and death compound his guilt
- FAILURE MODE: any reminder of having delivered another being to Galactus's service reopens the founding wound
- LEVERAGE: invoking her can extract concessions framed as making amends

### [[Thanos of Titan (The Mad Titan)]]
- Cosmic-scale adversary across multiple sagas; the Surfer is reliably the first to see and name the threat
- Mutual recognition; Thanos respects his witness even while opposing him
- FAILURE MODE: Thanos can offer cosmic-scale bargains (cessation of greater horror in exchange for compromise) that exploit the Surfer's moral arithmetic
- LEVERAGE (for analysts): Thanos's intelligence on the Surfer is high; track Thanos's reads as corroborating data

### Fantastic Four Defenders Avengers
- Courteous allies, never integrated; he stands beside but not within teams
- FAILURE MODE: prolonged team embedding produces withdrawal episodes; he renounces belonging by reflex
- LEVERAGE: appeals routed through the FF specifically (origin-of-rupture) land harder than from other teams
